# Historical Yamato/Japanese characters 1000008700-1000010699, 1000011900-1000012299
# First unused index: 1000012293

# Swap from Yamato to Japanese around 800-850 (for the Imperial Family, it would be the children of Junna and Ninmyo), but let people alive at that point remain Yamato since it is a parent culture and thus not a cause for rebellion

##### Added clans

# - Imperial Family
# - Fujiwara
# - Minamoto
# - Taira
# - Tachibana

# - Abe

##### The Imperial Family

# People before Emperor Keitai have been skipped
# All of these should have the amaterasu_descendant trait
# Includes people that later founded Minamoto/Taira/Tachibana branches, but not their descendants

### Emperor Keitai (1000008700) and his children (that have at least one verifiable date)

1000008700 = {
	name = "Ohodo" # Emperor Keitai
	dynasty = 1000027000 # Imperial Family
	religion = shinto
	culture = yamato
	trait = amaterasu_descendant
	450.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
	}
	# Married Princess Tashiraka (born 489), daughter of Emperor Ninken
	# Consorts:
	# - Owari Menokohime,daughter of Owari Kusaka)
	# - Mio Wakakohime,younger sister of Mio Tsunoori)
	# - Hirohime, daughter of Prince Sakata
	# - Okinaga Omino, daughter of Okinaga Mate
	# - Manda Sekihime, daughter of Manda Omochi
	# - Mio Yamatohime, daughter of Mio Katahi
	# - Wani Haehime, daughter of Wani Kawachi
	# - Hirohime, daughter of Ne
	507.3.3 = {
		name = "Keitai"
	}
	531.3.10 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

		name = "Ankan"
	}

		death = yes
	}
}

		birth = yes
	}

	# - Princess Nukatabe, daughter of Emperor Kinmei
	569.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000008710 # Before 570
	}
	# - Kasuga Ominako, daughter of Kasuga Nakakimi
	# - Unako Otoshi, daughter of Ohoka no Obito no Okuma
	571.4.30 = {
		name = "Bidatsu"
	}

			ROOT = {
				remove_consort = 1000008710
			}
		}
		add_spouse = 1000008710
	}
	585.9.14 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

### Children of Emperor Saga (1000008797) with at least one date

1000008838 = {
	name = "Masara" # Emperor Ninmyo
	dynasty = 1000027000 # Imperial Family
	religion = shinto
	culture = japanese
	trait = amaterasu_descendant
	father = 1000008797 # Emperor Saga
	mother = 1000010568 # Tachibana Kachiko
	trait = child_of_consort
	trait = twin
	810.12.1 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			set_character_flag = emperor_ninmyo
		}
	}
	# Married Fujiwara Nobuko, daughter of Fujiwara Fuyutsugu
	826.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = 1000009625 # Date unknown, but they had a son in 827
	}
	# Consorts:
	# - Fujiwara Sawako, daughter of Fujiwara Fusatsugu
	827.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000009507 # Unknown; they had a child in 828
	}
	# - Fujiwara Sadako, daughter of Fujiwara Mimori
	835.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000009400 # Unclear date, but they had a child in 836
	}
	# - Shigeno Tsunako, daughter of Shigeno Sadanushi
	828.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000012126 # Date unknown
	}
	# - Tachibana Kageko, daughter of Tachibana Ujikimi
	840.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = 1000010573 # Date unknown
	}
	# - Fujiwara Musuko
	# - Ki Taneko, daughter of Ki Natora
	834.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000012013 # Unknown
	}
	# - A woman from the Mikuni clan
	# - Fujiwara Katoko, daughter of Fujiwara Fukutomaro
	# - Fujiwara Warawako, daughter of Fujiwara Michito
	# - Princess Takamune, daughter of Prince Okaya
	# - A woman from the Yamaguchi clan
	# - Daughter of Kudara Toyofuku
	# - Kudara Yokyo, daughter of Kudara Kyofuku/Kyoshun; Wikipedia lists her separately from the above
	829.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000012210 # Date unknown
	}
	833.3.30 = {
		name = "Ninmyo"
		effect = {
			set_character_flag = emperor_ninmyo_used # If deposed, don't reuse the name!
		}
	}
	850.5.6 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

	dynasty = 1000027000 # Imperial Family

	trait = ambitious # Schemed to regain the throne

	1180.8.6 = {

			set_character_flag = emperor_toba
		}
	}

	1185.4.25 = {

		add_trait = under_regency

			set_character_flag = emperor_toba_used # If deposed, don't reuse the name!
		}
	}
	# Married Fujiwara Takako/Kujo Ninshi, daughter of Kujo Kanezane
	# Consorts:
	# - Minamoto Ariko, daughter of a priest named Noen and adoptive daughter of Minamoto Michitaka

	}

				add_claim = PREV
			}

				add_claim = PREV

				add_claim = PREV
